          (norm_ca): LayerNorm((768,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
          (cross_attn): MultiheadAttention(
            (out_proj): NonDynamicallyQuantizableLinear(in_features=768, out_features=768, bias=True)
          )
          (norm_prompts): LayerNorm((768,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
          (mlp_prompts): Mlp(
            (fc1): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=3072, bias=True)
            (act): GELU(approximate='none')
            (fc2): Linear(in_features=3072, out_features=768, bias=True)
            (drop): Dropout(p=0.0, inplace=False)
          )
        )
      )
    )
    (avd): AVD(
      (adaptive_view_disentangle): ModuleList(
        (0): ModuleDict(
          (mlp_cls_token): Mlp(
            (fc1): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=3072, bias=True)
            (act): GELU(approximate='none')
            (fc2): Linear(in_features=3072, out_features=768, bias=True)
            (drop): Dropout(p=0.0, inplace=False)
          )
          (norm_mask_1): LayerNorm((768,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
          (cross_attn): MultiheadAttention(
            (out_proj): NonDynamicallyQuantizableLinear(in_features=768, out_features=768, bias=True)
          )
          (norm_mask_2): LayerNorm((768,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
          (mlp_mask): Mlp(
            (fc1): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=3072, bias=True)
            (act): GELU(approximate='none')
            (fc2): Linear(in_features=3072, out_features=768, bias=True)
            (drop): Dropout(p=0.0, inplace=False)
          )
        )
      )
      (norm_sa): LayerNorm((768,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (self_attn): MultiheadAttention(
        (out_proj): NonDynamicallyQuantizableLinear(in_features=768, out_features=768, bias=True)
      )
      (norm_inv): LayerNorm((768,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (feature_enhance_mlp): Mlp(

        (drop): Dropout(p=0.0, inplace=False)
      )
      (norm_inv_enhance): LayerNorm((768,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    )
  )
  (ArctanLoss): RobustArctanLoss()
  (view_invariant_head): EmbeddingHead(
    (pool_layer): Identity()
    (bottleneck): Sequential(

          (norm_ca): LayerNorm((768,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
          (cross_attn): MultiheadAttention(
            (out_proj): NonDynamicallyQuantizableLinear(in_features=768, out_features=768, bias=True)
          )
          (norm_prompts): LayerNorm((768,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
          (mlp_prompts): Mlp(
            (fc1): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=3072, bias=True)
            (act): GELU(approximate='none')
            (fc2): Linear(in_features=3072, out_features=768, bias=True)
            (drop): Dropout(p=0.0, inplace=False)
          )
        )
      )
    )
    (avd): AVD(
      (adaptive_view_disentangle): ModuleList(
        (0): ModuleDict(
          (mlp_cls_token): Mlp(
            (fc1): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=3072, bias=True)
            (act): GELU(approximate='none')
            (fc2): Linear(in_features=3072, out_features=768, bias=True)
            (drop): Dropout(p=0.0, inplace=False)
          )

          (cross_attn): MultiheadAttention(
            (out_proj): NonDynamicallyQuantizableLinear(in_features=768, out_features=768, bias=True)
          )

            (drop): Dropout(p=0.0, inplace=False)
          )
        )
      )
      (norm_sa): LayerNorm((768,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)

        (out_proj): NonDynamicallyQuantizableLinear(in_features=768, out_features=768, bias=True)
      )
      (norm_inv): LayerNorm((768,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)

    )
  )
